        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2017172280" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1560730417338586885"><blockquote>#1 Captive Prince ★★★★★<br/>#2 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2224258844' rel='nofollow noopener'>Prince's Gambit</a> ★★★★★<br/>#3 <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2224259527' rel='nofollow noopener'>King's Rising</a> ★★★★★</blockquote><br/><b>3rd read update, june 2019:</b> I love this series more and more every single time I read it. ♥<br/><br/><b>original review, december 2017:</b><br/>Let me begin this review by saying that these are just my opinions and I am, in no way, about to glorify rape or abuse. I am a survivor myself, and I'm fully aware that this book bothered a <i>lot</i> of people. I would never question another reader's rating of this book, though, and I'm just going to ask you guys </span>
  <span id="freeText1560730417338586885" style="display:none"><blockquote>#1 Captive Prince ★★★★★<br />#2 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2224258844" rel="nofollow noopener">Prince's Gambit</a> ★★★★★<br />#3 <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2224259527" rel="nofollow noopener">King's Rising</a> ★★★★★</blockquote><br /><b>3rd read update, june 2019:</b> I love this series more and more every single time I read it. ♥<br /><br /><b>original review, december 2017:</b><br />Let me begin this review by saying that these are just my opinions and I am, in no way, about to glorify rape or abuse. I am a survivor myself, and I'm fully aware that this book bothered a <i>lot</i> of people. I would never question another reader's rating of this book, though, and I'm just going to ask you guys to extend the same courtesy. ❤<br /><br /><b>This book is NOT for everyone.</b> It involves a lot of rape, sexual violence and slavery, abuse, pedophilia, and various other incredibly uncomfortable topics. I can fully understand why someone would NOT enjoy this book, but I loved it.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>A golden prince was easy to love if you did not have to watch him picking wings off flies.</i>
</blockquote><br />I had no idea that it would be able to pack so much character- and world-building into such a short little story, or that it would be so <b>political</b>! Betrayal stories are some of my absolute favorites, so this was solid for me in that aspect, too.<br /><br />Not only did I enjoy the story line, but Damen/Damianos is such an enjoyable narrator and I felt so sorry for him, constantly. He makes some really poor choices at times, but he's genuinely got a heart of gold. He comes from a country where "slaves" are treated less like property and more like what we would consider sugar babies in our society, so watching adjust to the terrible ways the Veretians view their slaves and "pets" is a tough journey. I loved how true to himself he stayed, regardless of how miserable his circumstances were.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>This place sickened him. Anywhere else, you simply killed your enemy with a sword. Or poisoned him, if you had the honourless instincts of an assassin. Here, it was layer upon layer of constructed double-dealing, dark, polished, and unpleasant.</i>
</blockquote><br />Of course, Damen is the <i>only</i> genuinely likable main character in this story, and all other prominent figures are raging douchebags, but there are a few lovable side characters (like sweet little Erasmus), or minor characters that are terrible but pitiable (looking at you, Nicaise). Honestly, the complexity and terrible nature of most of the characters reminded me of GRRM's writing, where almost everyone is just totally despicable.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>"I'm not surprised you've driven three men to kill you, I'm only surprised there weren't more," said Damen, bluntly.</i>
</blockquote><br />All in all, please know what you're going into before picking this book up, and if you're triggered by rape descriptions and abuse scenarios in books, please, do <i>not</i> pick this up unless you know you're in the right head space for it. If you think you can handle it, though, and enjoy stories of political intrigue/royalty/betrayal etc., I highly recommend this series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1560730417338586885" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer383439798" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4780684014587341917"> <b>Compelling Reading...I was totally engrossed from start to finish....5 Fabulous Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1166.photobucket.com/albums/q618/Monique_Lehane/?action=view&current=Philip-Damon-Baker-Homotography-1.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386340i/745793._SX540_.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Captive Prince, literally captivated me! this is amazing storytelling and I can honestly say I picked it up to read and did not put it down until both book 1 and book 2 were finished.....it was 5am, but I was hooked! These 2 books are FREE, yes, can you believe it, such a great story is free to read. The only down side is that there is no news on book 3 yet, however I have noticed that she will be publishin</span>
  <span id="freeText4780684014587341917" style="display:none"> <b>Compelling Reading...I was totally engrossed from start to finish....5 Fabulous Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s1166.photobucket.com/albums/q618/Monique_Lehane/?action=view&amp;current=Philip-Damon-Baker-Homotography-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380386340i/745793._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Captive Prince, literally captivated me! this is amazing storytelling and I can honestly say I picked it up to read and did not put it down until both book 1 and book 2 were finished.....it was 5am, but I was hooked! These 2 books are FREE, yes, can you believe it, such a great story is free to read. The only down side is that there is no news on book 3 yet, however I have noticed that she will be publishing books 1 and 2 shortly in ebook and paperback, with added scenes, so 3 should not be too far behind and I would gladly pay good money for it. <br><br>We see this wonderful story unfold from Damen's perspective and it is full of political struggles, atrocious acts of violence and sex (these scenes are not graphic in nature), decadent entertainment, battles, intrigues and mysteries, but it all revolves around Power and the mind games and tactics of the players and pawns. You are constantly riveted to the action and unsure of the direction to which it will next take you. It is unpredictable and not a minute is wasted in this book.<br><br>Our two main characters Crown Prince Damianos of Akielos and Crown Prince Laurent of Rabat are pitched right in the middle of the unfolding events and action, they overcome their hatred of each other to tolerate one another and eventually to become friends and confidants. The sexual tension between these two leaves you constantly on the edge, to the point of frustration.......but Ooooh so worth the wait.<br><br>The story flows seamlessly and the world building is full of warring Kingdoms, beautiful landscapes and an array of colours, decadent buildings filled with opulence on a grand scale and beautiful people with adorned pets/sex slaves bedecked in gold and jewels. Ohhhh and the characters, easily recognised with their personalities and individual voices, my favourite being Laurant, so cool and aloof, with graceful beauty and an air of contempt, arrogant and nefarious in his actions, with each nuance and idiosyncrasy so clear in my minds eye...he is definitely an enigma.<br><br><b>This is a fabulous read, I loved it and I happily recommend it to all of my friends, well...those that have not already had the pleasure of reading it and are also waiting with baited breath for the next book!</b><br><br><i>For more reviews, please visit...</i><a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/?zx=fa7d78fe43e1074" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11227380184634037703">Buddy Reread March 2019. Loved it even more. <br/><br/><b>5++++++++ stars</b><br/><br/>Oh dear Lord, Zeus, Poseidon and Thor forgive me because I actually loved this book. The book does not shy away from sensitive subjects like rape, slavery, flogging, public humiliation. And yet I could not stop reading it, and the writing was sooo goood!, this book got my attention from page 1.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500273479ra/23316220.gif' width='400' height='230' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Before you read just know that when they refer to a pet, they don’t mean a cute dog or a sassy lazy cat that sleeps all day and looks at you with</span>
  <span id="freeText11227380184634037703" style="display:none">Buddy Reread March 2019. Loved it even more. <br><br><b>5++++++++ stars</b><br><br>Oh dear Lord, Zeus, Poseidon and Thor forgive me because I actually loved this book. The book does not shy away from sensitive subjects like rape, slavery, flogging, public humiliation. And yet I could not stop reading it, and the writing was sooo goood!, this book got my attention from page 1.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500273479ra/23316220.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Before you read just know that when they refer to a pet, they don’t mean a cute dog or a sassy lazy cat that sleeps all day and looks at you with judgmental eyes, Nope pets are people!<br> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1500273479ra/23316221.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <i>
  <b>‘He doesn’t look much like a pet,’ said the taller of the two men.<br> ‘You heard. He’s a bed slave from Akielos,’ said the other.<br> ‘You think the Prince fucks him?’ Sceptically.<br> ‘More like the other way around.’<br> ‘Pretty sweet orders for a bed slave.’ The taller’s mind stuck on the subject as the other<br> grunted noncommittally in reply. ‘Think what that’d be like, getting a leg over the Prince.’<br> I imagine it would be a lot like lying down with a poisonous snake, thought Damen, but he<br> kept the thought to himself.</b>
</i><br><br>Laurent - this guy is a manipulative son of a gun, he is a sadist, he likes mind games, i wanted to hate him but nope I actually loved him.<br><br> <i>
  <b>“Is ambition needed in a king?” said Laurent. “Or is it simply needed to become king?”</b>
</i><br><br>Damien oh you sweet poor man, i wanted him to be free, i liked that he tried to fight back and did not just let the veretians bring him down easily, and he has a mouth that sometimes just could not shut up to save his life.<br><br> <i>
  <b>The words came out before he could stop them. ‘I speak your language better than you speak mine, sweetheart</b>
</i><br><br>Oh and Nicaise you little bastard, i felt sorry for him and at the same time i wanted him gone, but i kinda like him and I think that Laurent has a soft spot for him from the way they interacted.<br><br>Definitely going continue with these series. I can't believe i loved it even though there is zero romance...hmmm!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1447559239ra/17021797.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Laurent's uncle..... <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1496022067ra/22875104.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15854935071903848675"><br/>Readers,what do I say about this book??<br/><br/><i>
  <b>Power. Brilliance. Excellence. All delivered in one perfect package.</b>

  <span id="freeText15854935071903848675" style="display:none"><br />Readers,what do I say about this book??<br /><br /><i>
  <b>Power. Brilliance. Excellence. All delivered in one perfect package.</b>
</i><br /><br /><pre>
  <b>This is fiction at its finest!!!</b>
</pre><br /><i>Captive Prince.....</i><br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>This is what they mean when they say that a book has the ability to transport you to worlds beyond!!</b>
</i><br /><br /><i>And was I ever???</i><br /><br />This one gripped me in it's powerful clutches,and did not let go.This is what I look for in a book.<br /><br /><b>This book entranced,enchanted and devoured me.</b><br /><br />And I loved every minute of it!!<br /><br />---------------------------------------------------------<br /><br />Damianos is Crown Prince of Akielos.Rightful heir to his father's throne.But then is caught in the plotting of his half brother.Overnight,he loses everything....<br /><br /><b>His kingdom,his freedom and his very identity.</b><br /><br />He is then gifted to the Crown Prince of Rabat as a <b>pleasure slave</b>.Once an enemy nation,now a tremulous treaty exists between them.<br /><br /><i>And then it all starts.</i><br /><br /><b>The true tests of bravery,courage and honour.</b><br /><br />And what captured me the most??<br /><br /><b>The beauty,which shone even brighter in the face of all the brutality!!</b><br /><br /><br /><i>And what I did not like......</i><br /><br />Ummm....,errrrr....,nothing!!Seriously,I loved everything about it!!<br /><br /><br />It captured my heart!!I wish I could have told you more,but frankly,I won't be able to do it justice.<br /><br />-----------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>Note to Readers--</b><br /><br />I know that for many of you this premise is a big no.Slavery,brutality,the darkness.I understand.But still,I will ask all of you to give this a chance.I absolutely loved it.<br /><br /><b>READ IT!!!</b><br /><br />You may not fall in love with it like me,but then again,you may!<br /><br />You'll never know unless you try.<br /><br /><br /><b>That's all for now,Readers.<br /><br />Ta-Ta!!</b><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_1385092471" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1385092471" />
    <a title="Samantha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10067920-samantha"><img alt="Samantha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590018789p2/10067920.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1385092471?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Samantha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Samantha" href="/user/show/10067920-samantha">Samantha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1385092471" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17148385920857805051">I neither loved nor hated this book and I was surprised about that since it tends to bring out very strong emotions in people. <br/><br/>I'm going to be doing a full review on this book, but wanted to touch on a few things here since it is such a controversial read. <br/><br/>Firstly, I've always planned on reading this entire series regardless of if I hated the first book. Especially because this series should honestly just be one book. All of the books are short enough to combine. <br/><br/>Secondly, yes OBVIOUSLY trigger </span>
  <span id="freeText17148385920857805051" style="display:none">I neither loved nor hated this book and I was surprised about that since it tends to bring out very strong emotions in people. <br /><br />I'm going to be doing a full review on this book, but wanted to touch on a few things here since it is such a controversial read. <br /><br />Firstly, I've always planned on reading this entire series regardless of if I hated the first book. Especially because this series should honestly just be one book. All of the books are short enough to combine. <br /><br />Secondly, yes OBVIOUSLY trigger warnings for rape, abuse, pedophilia, etc. Most people know that going in by now. And maybe I was over prepared, but this book isn't nearly as brutal as I was prepared for it to be. If you don't have those warnings before going in, maybe it is. But not as bad as I was expecting. Yes, the world is very different than ours. All of the countries have slaves. All of the countries have pleasure slaves. Rape is a prominent thing. But there is definitely more grey area and room for discussion of consent in this world than one might think going in, and that's probably why opinions on this series are so black and white. <br /><br />Lastly, THIS BOOK IS NOT A ROMANCE. Now that all books are out, we know that's the direction it goes. But there is no romance in this book at all. I'm actually really interested to see how this series goes about its redemption arcs and how so many people come to love Laurent. Because yeah, he's an asshole. So what is done to possibly redeem him?!? I'm intrigued to see how that is attempted and if it is successful in my eyes, because I'm super skeptical. <br /><br />The writing in this is nothing to write home about. It's definitely over the top at times and stumbles into "fanfiction AU" territory with some of its tropes. But it is very easy to read because of that. <br /><br />That was a lot more than I planned on writing but oh well. I'm committed to the rest of this series so we'll see which side I land on in the end. </span>
  <a data-text-id="17148385920857805051" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

of sexual coercion?<br>Well,there's none of that,in fact there's ..<br><br>No romance<br>It's not erotic<br>But there is a very hedonistic feel to the book.<br><br>I'll keep this brief because there are already some fantastic reviews out there.<br><br>Damen is the heir to the throne of Akielos and is captured and given as a gift to Prince Laurent,heir to the kingdom of Vere.<br>Damen has been with men and women but Laurent's sexuality is definitely a mystery.<br><br>There is hardly any sex on page <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and none between the two main characters <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> and it is a bit violent in places with scenes of rape( but not too graphic,imo )<br><br>I think this first book was more scene setting and story building of what was to come.These two men obviously hate each other initially,coming from rival Kingdoms.<br>There is sexual tension of sorts but more on the part of Damen as the book is only from his pov.<br><br>So was the hype about this book justified??<br>Most definitely.The writing and the characters are so compelling.<br>I'm currently reading book two and loving Damen and Laurent..</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="7699952720178800809" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2109099269" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2109099269" />
    <a title="Shin Mon Thway" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/69053579-shin-mon-thway"><img alt="Shin Mon Thway" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504764254p2/69053579.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2109099269?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shin Mon Thway" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shin Mon Thway" href="/user/show/69053579-shin-mon-thway">Shin Mon Thway</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/35524380-captive-prince">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69053579-shin-mon-thway?shelf=fantasy-world">fantasy-world</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69053579-shin-mon-thway?shelf=master-slave-mm">master-slave-mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69053579-shin-mon-thway?shelf=fantasy-world-romance">fantasy-world-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69053579-shin-mon-thway?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69053579-shin-mon-thway?shelf=mm-romance">mm-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69053579-shin-mon-thway?shelf=virgins-mm">virgins-mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69053579-shin-mon-thway?shelf=favorites-mm">favorites-mm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69053579-shin-mon-thway?shelf=definitely-reread">definitely-reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69053579-shin-mon-thway?shelf=deliciously-dirty">deliciously-dirty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/69053579-shin-mon-thway?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2109099269" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9306026411671816284"><b>Reread: 7th June 2018<br/><br/>Oh, what I wouldn’t give to relive this story for the very first time again. 😌 Laurent and Damen are the perfect epitome of my book boyfriends’ standards. 😍 The plotting, scheming, treachery, spying, danger, love, romance, suspense and a mystery, this trilogy has it all. No wonder it was considered one of the greatest MM fantasy romance trilogy of all times. 👏 D&L still certainly is my all time favorite couple. If I could only wish one thing and it would come true, I’d certa</b></span>
  <span id="freeText9306026411671816284" style="display:none"><b>Reread: 7th June 2018<br><br>Oh, what I wouldn’t give to relive this story for the very first time again. 😌 Laurent and Damen are the perfect epitome of my book boyfriends’ standards. 😍 The plotting, scheming, treachery, spying, danger, love, romance, suspense and a mystery, this trilogy has it all. No wonder it was considered one of the greatest MM fantasy romance trilogy of all times. 👏 D&amp;L still certainly is my all time favorite couple. If I could only wish one thing and it would come true, I’d certainly wish to be Laurent and have a happily ever after with sweet sweet Damianos. *happy sigh* 😌 Well now, I’m certainly high on D&amp;L. 😍<br><br><br><br><br>ORIGINAL REVIEW (A bit revised after a reread) </b><br><br><br>I don't have much to say in this review except that it's extremely well plotted and written because this is only the first book of the trilogy and the story is still blossoming. <b>(That's what I thought when I started writing this review and you can see how wrong I was! 😂)</b><br><br>So we have two extraordinary MCs in this fantastic story, the former crown prince of Akielos, Damianos and now a pleasure slave called Damen and the current crown prince of Vera, Laurent. These two men are archenemies since Damen killed Laurent's older brother in a battle that happened 6 years ago. When Damen's father, the king Theomedes, passed away, his half-brother Kastor seized the crown and sent Damen to Vera as a pleasure slave to serve the crown prince, Laurent. Laurent didn't know the true identity of Damen <b>(perhaps .. or may be he's just pretending not to know. 😉)</b> and just thought of him as a barbaric uncontrollable slave. And since Laurent certainly have no love lost for Akielos, the relationship dynamic between Laurent and Damen is extremely difficult to say the least. <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528381574i/25680231._SX540_.jpg" width="height=" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510860940i/24462145._SY540_.jpg" width="height=" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>Things are getting very interesting since Laurent is facing with a very similar fate with Damen since his uncle, the current regent of Vera, covets his nephew's throne. And now with Laurent sent off to Delfeur, the boarder between Vera and Akielos, to conveniently die and open a door for his uncle to finally ascend the throne officially, we will now have to wait and see what will happen in the next book and how these two men will collaborate together to win their rightful thrones. With a spark of epic romance of course! 😉<br><br><br><br>So here's a few things you need to know.<br><br><i>1. This story is unlike other MM romance novels in this genre filled with fun and fluffy romance and a casual storyline. This is a very heavily and intricately plotted novel. <br><br>2. It's a bit hard to catch up with all the names of the characters and the cities since it's based in an alternative fantasy universe and I'm extremely grateful that there's a glossary at the very beginning of the book. <br><br>3. You won't get steamy, hot and lusty smut in this book. At least, not between our two MCs. (I'm not sure about what will happen in the next books. 😁) Yes, there's some sex performance and wanton scenes in the story but not intended to stimulate your libido as in most romance novels. It simply was just a necessity to make the story more obscene, cruel and realistic. <br><br>4. This book is all about a fascinating story rather than a simple time-pass read and if you can't commit yourself to finish the trilogy, don't bother reading this first book because you won't get the authentic taste of these books. And this book certainly isn’t a standalone.</i><br><br><br><br>Overall, I immensely enjoyed this book and I can’t wait To dug into the remaining two books. 😌 I just wished I also got Laurent’s PoV rather than only getting Damen’s. It would be such an exquisite treat to get a peek inside that extraordinarily beautiful and complicated mind! 💙 I can't thank my babydoll <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4167077-al-the-serial-series-skipper" rel="nofollow noopener"><br>Al</a> enough for recommending these beautiful books. Love you gal!!! 😘<br><br><br>5 That is the fate of all princes destined for a throne stars </b><br>⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528382484i/25680320._SX540_.jpg" width="height=" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1528382484i/25680319._SY540_.jpg" width="height=" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1510860940i/24462146._SY540_.jpg" width="height=" alt="description/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9306026411671816284" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1064714643" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1064714643" />
    <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner"><img alt="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1532688964p2/31461418.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1064714643?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘" href="/user/show/31461418-alienor-french-frowner">Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Alienor ✘ French Frowner ✘ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/14596170-cristina-monica">Cristina Monica</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31461418-alienor-french-frowner?shelf=romance">romance</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1064714643" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12105440007733434511"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454765217i/18011641._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b><u>TRIGGER WARNING</u> : graphic violence, rape, slavery</b><br/><br/><b><u>4.5 stars</u>. Oh, the dilemma.</b> Review it? Jump on book 2? Review it? Jump on book 2? Review it? Jump on book 2? <br/><br/><i>Eenie meenie miney mo<br/>Catch a tiger by the toe<br/>If he hollars let him go<br/>Eenie meenie miney mo</i><br/><br/>Oh, <i>screw it</i>. I swear that I'll write a real review of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9305362.Captive_Prince__Captive_Prince___1_' title='Captive Prince (Captive Prince, #1) by C.S. Pacat' rel='nofollow noopener'>Captive Prince: Volume One</a> because <i>Helloooo</i>, it deserves ones, but for now my excitation and eagerness to freaking KNOW what will happen leads me to shorten my ramble and only give you reduced info</span>
  <span id="freeText12105440007733434511" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454765217i/18011641._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><u>TRIGGER WARNING</u> : graphic violence, rape, slavery</b><br><br><b><u>4.5 stars</u>. Oh, the dilemma.</b> Review it? Jump on book 2? Review it? Jump on book 2? Review it? Jump on book 2? <br><br><i>Eenie meenie miney mo<br>Catch a tiger by the toe<br>If he hollars let him go<br>Eenie meenie miney mo</i><br><br>Oh, <i>screw it</i>. I swear that I'll write a real review of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9305362.Captive_Prince__Captive_Prince___1_" title="Captive Prince (Captive Prince, #1) by C.S. Pacat" rel="nofollow noopener">Captive Prince: Volume One</a> because <i>Helloooo</i>, it deserves ones, but for now my excitation and eagerness to freaking KNOW what will happen leads me to shorten my ramble and only give you reduced information (perhaps that's for the best) (you don't want to read my entire rambling) (trust me)<br><br>☑ Welcome to a <b>harsh and unforgiving world where slavery (including sexual), torture and rape are common practice (including towards youngers, which makes the book so fucking hard to stomach at times)</b>. I know, I know, <i>YIKES</i>, but trust me, if I could handle it it's only thanks to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4349837.C_S__Pacat" title="C.S. Pacat" rel="nofollow noopener">C.S. Pacat</a>'s talent for dealing with these awful subjects without never showing any form of indulgence towards them. Indeed it's obvious from the start that <b>Damen, the MC, doesn't condone nor accept Vere's barbaric customs</b>. This said, he is the product of this world, therefore what is normal to him can appear quite horrible for our contemporary minds, and with reasons. If he hates people to be abused, he does accept slavery as normal - like a Roman would have. This does not mean that we readers are supposed to agree with him, but actually the opposite. Although I was trembling with rage as soon as I reached page two - and my sentiments never wavered - my fury was focused on this <b>world</b>, as I'm sure the author intended to. <br><br>☑ If the world-building leaves several shadow zones and can't be compared to the level of a full fantasy novel, in my opinion it wasn't the point : <b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9305362.Captive_Prince__Captive_Prince___1_" title="Captive Prince (Captive Prince, #1) by C.S. Pacat" rel="nofollow noopener">Captive Prince: Volume One</a> is character driven and the political machinations and cunning mostly made up for the relative lack of information about the 'outside' world.</b> Early on my mind was reeling, and despite the fact that I guessed several outcomes, it didn't diminished my enjoyment because - <br><br>Well, because -<br><br>☑ <b>Laurent. HOLY SHIT I CAN'T HATE HIM. He fascinates me way too much.</b> Perhaps I should feel ashamed, given the fact that he's a torturer son of a bitch for most of the novel but HEY! You're talking to the girl who loves <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9579634-prince-of-thorns?from_search=true&amp;search_version=service" rel="nofollow noopener">Jorg of Ancrath</a>. So there's that. You know you can't trust me when it comes to COMPLEX and straight on CAPTIVATING villains. I just can't. I'm sorry, blablabla, and all that. So, Laurent. He's harsh, manipulative, intransigent, secret, unwilling to trust, multi-layered, HE MADE ME LAUGH (because dry humor is somehow right up my alley. WOOT!) - <b>He also is growing. I cannot wait to see who he will become in the next books.</b> (to be taken literally) (on to book 2 right now)<br><br>☑ <b>The grow of Damen and Laurent's relationship is perfectly handled - there's no romance here, guys</b>. Also, banter. Banter is EVERYTHING. Especially when it's so subtle that every giggle comes with a gasp of surprise. <br><br>To conclude this review that is already way longer than I had expected (somehow it doesn't come as a surprise), I'll say that I was never bored - Not at <b>any moment</b>. Appalled, furious, captivated, curious, yes. Not bored.<br><br>► <b>This is quite a success. Color me surprised. No, scratch that : color me stunned instead</b>. Beware, <u>this does NOT mean that I would recommend this book to anyone. I WOULDN'T, because I'm not lying when I say that it's really REALLY harsh and morally questionable. Please go warned</u>.<br>________________________<br>► WHAT? This is just me jumping on the bandwagon :P<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454619276ra/17992673.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Thanks so much to my adorable friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/5312173-simona-bartolotta" rel="nofollow noopener">Simona</a> for the gift ♥</span>

<div id="review_1631544351" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1631544351" />
    <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover"><img alt="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489089790p2/34338862.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1631544351?book_show_action=true">May 07, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" class="user" itemprop="url" name="TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover" href="/user/show/34338862-thecrazyworldofabooklover">TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1631544351" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5982091577487495142"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“A golden prince was easy to love if you did not have to watch him picking wings off flies.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>If this book was a person it would be:<br/><br/><a href='http://s1270.photobucket.com/user/sturano555/media/jof_zpsyh0uau1j.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484360637ra/21712193.gif' alt=' photo jof_zpsyh0uau1j.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I mean. This book was full of depravity and brutality and cunning characters. And just plain ol'fucked up. <br/><br/>And what's worse? <br/><br/>I enjoyed it. A lot. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1270.photobucket.com/user/sturano555/media/17d1e2e9308a37bb412dbe31358da85b_zpsebacdmla.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484360637ra/21712194.gif' alt=' photo 17d1e2e9308a37bb412dbe31358da85b_zpsebacdmla.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>And at times, it was even quite funny. I laughed. Some parts were so twisted I really just couldn't help myself.<br/><br/><a href='http://s1270.photobucket.com/user/sturano555/media/wrong_zpse5wylh5h.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484360637ra/21712195.gif' alt=' photo wrong_zpse5wylh5h.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Let's get something straight. I don't enjoy the topics of slavery, torture, rape, sadism</span>
  <span id="freeText5982091577487495142" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“A golden prince was easy to love if you did not have to watch him picking wings off flies.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>If this book was a person it would be:<br><br><a href="http://s1270.photobucket.com/user/sturano555/media/jof_zpsyh0uau1j.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484360637ra/21712193.gif" alt=" photo jof_zpsyh0uau1j.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I mean. This book was full of depravity and brutality and cunning characters. And just plain ol'fucked up. <br><br>And what's worse? <br><br>I enjoyed it. A lot. <br><br><a href="http://s1270.photobucket.com/user/sturano555/media/17d1e2e9308a37bb412dbe31358da85b_zpsebacdmla.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484360637ra/21712194.gif" alt=" photo 17d1e2e9308a37bb412dbe31358da85b_zpsebacdmla.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And at times, it was even quite funny. I laughed. Some parts were so twisted I really just couldn't help myself.<br><br><a href="http://s1270.photobucket.com/user/sturano555/media/wrong_zpse5wylh5h.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1484360637ra/21712195.gif" alt=" photo wrong_zpse5wylh5h.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Let's get something straight. I don't enjoy the topics of slavery, torture, rape, sadism. In spite of my sometimes awful potty mouth, I'm a little bit of a prude. *winks*. So I was kind of nervous to read a story that has the reputation this book has. <br><br>But..this author. She took some really awful topics, some downright shitty characters, and made them <b>so freaking engaging and interesting that I COULD NOT PUT THIS DOWN.</b><br><br>Quick summary: Damen, Prince of Akielos, is betrayed by his half brother and sold to the enemy land of Vere. Once there, he's forced to act as a slave to the revenge thirsty, sadistic Prince Laurent who hates Damen's country and everything it stands for. <br><br><i>Laurent.</i> Oh, Laurent. I was so excited to meet this character dubbed as one of the most evil characters out there. And he did not disappoint. I could use so many words to describe him: <i>Asshole. Sadisitic. Viscous. Calculating. OUT OF HIS FUCKING MIND.</i> But the fact that I actually grew to <b>LIKE</b> Laurent is really just a testament to the author's clever and impressive writing skills. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>‘I can end this any time I like?’ said Laurent. ‘I haven’t even begun.’</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>What happens after, I won't get into. But Captive Prince clearly sets the foundation for the books to come. The relationship between Laurent and Damen, the fantastic writing, and all of the political intrigue left me wanting MORE, so I'm off to read book two like right this second!<br><br>**I clearly enjoyed this, <b>but I'm fully aware this book isn't for everyone.</b> The writing is <b>fantastic.</b> (Really. You can claim the events in this are horrid, and I'll agree. But no-one can say this woman's writing is not beyond. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/556801950?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">This review</a> explains it so perfectly.) I can see how it would be hard far some to follow, especially with the many difficult names and characters that are introduced. I wouldn't recommend it to anyone sensitive to or uncomfortable with upsetting stories and non-consensual sexual encounters. Also, this is categorized as romance, but there wasn't any in <i>this</i> installment. Don't go into this one expecting any sort of lovey dovey feelings, because you won't be getting any. It's clear there will be romance in the upcoming books, though, and <b>I CAN'T WAIT</b> to see how that unfolds.<br><br><br><a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com/" target="blog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467902722i/19644381._SX540_.jpg" width="275" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>Find Me On:<br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/thecrazyworldofabooklover/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/profile.php?id=100009277089211" rel="nofollow noopener">FB Page</a> ❤ <a href="https://www.facebook.com/TheCrazyWorldOfABookLover/" rel="nofollow noopener">FB Blog</a> ❤ <a href="https://thecrazyworldofabooklover.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> ❤ <a href="https://twitter.com/_StephDeMarco_" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a></span>

<div id="review_470695761" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/470695761" />
    <a title="Susan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/739211-susan"><img alt="Susan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1335133091p2/739211.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/470695761?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Susan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Susan" href="/user/show/739211-susan">Susan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer470695761" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15276008650574643326"><br/><b>OBSESSED.</b> <-me.<br/><br/>Captive Prince (Vol. 1) took the sharpest hook it could find and dug it deep into me and just pulled me along wherever it wanted to go.<br/><br/><u>The writing:</u> phenomenal<br/><u>The world-building:</u> detailed & fascinating<br/><u>The characters:</u> deliciously layered<br/><u>The story:</u> political intrigue and mind-fuckery at its best<br/><br/>I was in a mild haze of confusion some of the time…there are a LOT of characters and countries and deceptive alliances and loyalties. But, if you just play along, it all starts to make sense a</span>
  <span id="freeText15276008650574643326" style="display:none"><br /><b>OBSESSED.</b> &lt;-me.<br /><br />Captive Prince (Vol. 1) took the sharpest hook it could find and dug it deep into me and just pulled me along wherever it wanted to go.<br /><br /><u>The writing:</u> phenomenal<br /><u>The world-building:</u> detailed &amp; fascinating<br /><u>The characters:</u> deliciously layered<br /><u>The story:</u> political intrigue and mind-fuckery at its best<br /><br />I was in a mild haze of confusion some of the time…there are a LOT of characters and countries and deceptive alliances and loyalties. But, if you just play along, it all starts to make sense and is knit together into an intricate weave of something…something fantastic. <br /><br />The story is a chess match with everyone thinking 3 moves ahead and me wondering what just happened in the last move! <i>(a little slow, this one…*points at self*)</i><br /><br />But Volume 1 left me wanting more. I need explanations and more details and I need to know what happens of heroic Damen and brilliant Laurant (&lt;-one of the best “bad guys” I’ve read in a long time…reminds me of Carnac from The Administration)<br /><br />Yes, it’s a WIP and that made me hesitate to start for awhile. But honestly, don’t delay. It’s too good to pass up…<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15276008650574643326" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('tdsT+dpCTqE+9Kf6gXVDaMUjUPAvdml6zQ2z+rTIYOzIG/ixgl80d4Xk02KaR6R3cXdSkU/+AADOq9b5r/Jyow==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pl7elXG520F8Ku9WV5kPmyUVyIrduY/tJiFakYO0N9nbnjXdKaShl8c6m85Mq+iEkUHK670x5pclhz+SmI4llg==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer7276427475698040306">C.S. Pacat is a Melbourne writer. Her first series the <i>Captive Prince</i> trilogy began its life as an original web serial. Self-published in 2013 to critical and commercial success and acclaim, the <i>Captive Prince</i> trilogy was acquired by Penguin, and will be published worldwide in 2015.<br/></span>

</div>
